Update: - We had a pretty huge bug in our class changes that caused a bunch of errors. This is now fixed, sorry for the scare/inconvenience! ><

Mists of Pandaria Beta - Patch 15640
A new beta patch went up tonight, and there are a lot of changes. Keep checking back, as our list isn't complete just yet!

Tier 14 Set Bonuses

Spell Changes
http://static.mmo-champion.com/mmoc/images/icons/ideathknights.gif Death Knight (Forums (http://www.mmo-champion.com/forums/269-Death-Knight))
Baseline

Death Coil (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/47541/#15589-15640) now costs 35 Runic power, down from 40.
Death Grip (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/49576/#15589-15640) now has a 25 sec cooldown, down from 35.
Necrotic Strike (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/73975/#15589-15640) now slows casting speed by 50% on creatures and 25% on players instead of a flat 30%.

Talents

Anti-Magic Zone (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/51052/#15589-15640) base absorb has been increased by 1000%, now scales from 400% of Strength instead of 200% of Attack Power.
Blood Tap (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/45529/#15589-15640) now generates up to 12 charges, up from 10.
Death Siphon (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/108196/#15589-15640) damage has been reduced by 33%. Now scales from 40% of AP, down from 60%. Now heals for 100% of the damage dealt, up from 75%.
Death's Advance (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/96268/#15589-15640) now causes movement-impairing effects to not reduce you below 100% of normal speed, up from 75%.
Desecrated Ground (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/108201/#15589-15640) no longer deals damage.
Gorefiend's Grasp (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/108199/#15589-15640) no longer deals damage.
Purgatory [NYI] (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/114556/#15589-15640) *New* - An unholy pacts grants you the ability to fight on through damage that would kill mere mortals. When you would sustain fatal damage, you instead are wrapped in a Shroud of Purgatory, absorbing incoming healing equal to the amount of damage prevented, lasting 3 sec. If Shroud of Purgatory runs its course, you die. If it is removed through healing before its expiration, you survive. This effect may only occur every 2 minutes.
Lichborne (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/49039/#15589-15640) now causes Death Coil to heal you.
Plague Leech (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/123693/#15589-15640) *New* - Draw forth the infection from an enemy, consuming your Blood Plague and Frost Fever diseases on the target to activate a random fully-depleted rune as a Death Rune. 30 yd range, Instant, 25 sec cooldown.

Unholy

Ebon Plaguebringer (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/51160/#15589-15640) now also increases the damage your diseases deal by 60%.

Blood

Veteran of the Third War (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/50029/#15589-15640) no longer reduces the cooldown of Outbreak.

Glyphs

Glyph of Outbreak (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/59332/#15589-15640) - Your Outbreak spell no longer has a cooldown, but now costs 40 Runic Power.


http://static.mmo-champion.com/mmoc/images/icons/idruids.gif Druid (Forums (http://www.mmo-champion.com/forums/270-Druid))
Baseline

Ferocious Bite (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/22568/#15589-15640) now scales from 111.5% of AP at 5 Combo Points, up from 69% of AP.
Frenzied Regeneration (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/22842/#15589-15640) now heals up to 250% of AP health.
Lacerate (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/33745/#15589-15640) now scales from 82.2% of Attack Power with no base damage instead of base damage + 38.6% of Attack Power. DoT now deals 68.2% of Attack Power with no base damage instead of 51.6% of AP + base damage.
Mangle (Bear) (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/33878/#15589-15640) now deals 470% weapon damage instead of 350% damage and additional bonus damage.
Mangle (Cat) (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/33876/#15589-15640) now deals 480% damage, up from 370% damage.
Maul (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/6807/#15589-15640) now scales from 110% weapon damage instead of 100% weapon damage plus additional bonus damage.
Moonfire (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/8921/#15589-15640) DoT base damage has been reduced by 33%. Now scales from 24.8% of Spell Power, up from 22.7%. Now deals damage over 12 seconds instead of 18 seconds.
Ravage! (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/102545/#15589-15640) now deals 850% damage, up from 650%.
Starfall (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/50288/#15589-15640) now scales from 34% of Spell Power, up from 31.2%.
Swipe (Cat) (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/62078/#15589-15640) now awards 1 combo points if it strikes your current combo target.
Thrash (Bear) (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/77758/#15589-15640) direct damage now scales from 20.3% of Attack Power with no additional damage. DoT damage now scales from 93.6% of Attack Power with no additional damage.
Wrath (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/5176/#15589-15640) now scales from 121% of Spell Power, up from 110%.

Talents

Force of Nature (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/106737/#15589-15640) now has a 60 sec cooldown and lasts 15 secs instead of a 3 min cooldown and a 1 min duration.
Heart of the Wild (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/108288/#15589-15640) now depends on which specs you're NOT, instead of which spec you are.

Balance

Starfall (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/48505/#15589-15640) now scales from 34% of Spell Power, up from 31.2%.
Starfire (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/2912/#15589-15640) now scales from 169.4% of Spell Power, up from 155.3%

Feral

Ravage (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/6785/#15589-15640) now deals 850% damage, up from 650%.
Rip (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/1079/#15589-15640) now scales from 27.5% of Attack Power at 5 Combo Points, up from 21% of AP.
Shred (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/5221/#15589-15640) now deals 480% damage, up from 370%.

Guardian

Savage Defense (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/62606/#15589-15640) now has a 1.5 sec cooldown. Now increases change to dodge by 45%, up from 40%.


http://static.mmo-champion.com/mmoc/images/icons/ihunters.gif Hunter (Forums (http://www.mmo-champion.com/forums/271-Hunter))
Baseline

Arcane Shot (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/3044/#15589-15640) now costs 22 Focus, down from 25 Focus.

Talents

Call Beast (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/120679/#15589-15640) is now named Dire Beast (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/120679/#15589-15640).
Powershot (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/109259/#15589-15640) now has a 3 sec cast time, up from 1.5 sec. Now deals 400% weapon damage plus 100% weapon damage to all enemies in between you and the target. Up from 100% weapon damage + 25% to all enemies.
Silencing Shot (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/34490/#15589-15640) now has a 40 yards range, up from 35 yards.

Beast Mastery

Go for the Throat (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/34954/#15589-15640) has an additional effect: your Arcane Shot critical strikes reduce the Focus cost of your pet's next Basic Attack by 100% for 12 sec.
Kill Command (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/34026/#15589-15640) base damage has been increased by 12.5%

Marksmanship

Aimed Shot (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/19434/#15589-15640) now deals 160% ranged weapon damage, up from 90%. Additional damage increased by 100%.
Chimera Shot (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/53209/#15589-15640) now costs 44 Focus, down from 50% Focus.
Rapid Recuperation (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/53232/#15589-15640) no longer gives you Focus when you gain Rapid Killing.

Survival

Black Arrow (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/3674/#15589-15640) now costs 35 Focus, is Instant, and has a 30 sec cooldown. Black Arrow is now a DoT dealing 5,180 damage over 20 sec. Now shares a cooldown with other Fire Trap spells.
Explosive Shot (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/53301/#15589-15640) now costs 44 Focus, down from 50 Focus.
Lock and Load (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/56343/#15589-15640) now also procs from Explosive Trap.
Serpent Spread *New* (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/87935/#15589-15640) - Targets hit by your Multi-Shot are also afflicted by your Serpent Sting.
Trap Mastery (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/63458/#15589-15640) now also affects Black Arrow.

Glyphs

Glyph of Distracting Shot (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/123632/#15589-15640) - Your Distracting Shot now distracts the target to attack your pet instead of you.
Glyph of No Escape (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/53299/#15589-15640) no longer affects Ice Trap.
Growl (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/2649/#15589-15640) threat has been increased by 11%.


http://static.mmo-champion.com/mmoc/images/icons/images.gif Mage (Forums (http://www.mmo-champion.com/forums/272-Mage))
Baseline

Frostfire Bolt (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/44614/#15589-15640) now slows the target for 8 sec, down from 9 sec.
Mage Armor (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/6117/#15589-15640) now increases your Mastery by 2717 at Level 90.
Polymorph (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/61780/#15589-15640) (All versions) now has a 30 yards range, down from 35 yards.
Slow Fall (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/130/#15589-15640) no longer requires a reagent.

Talents

Invocation (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/114003/#15589-15640) now reduces the cooldown of Evocation to 10 sec.
Scorch (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/2948/#15589-15640) now costs 0.1% of Base Mana.
Temporal Shield (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/115610/#15589-15640) isn't on the global cooldown.

Frost

Brain Freeze (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/44549/#15589-15640) now causes your next Frostfire Bolt to be instant cast, cost no mana, deal 25% additional damage, and act as if your target were frozen for 15 sec.
Fingers of Frost (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/112965/#15589-15640) no has a 12% chance to proc from Frozen Orb hits, down from 20%. Now also has a 4% chance to proc from Blizzard ticks. Now has a 9% chance to proc from Scorch, up from 8%.
Frostbolt (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/116/#15589-15640) now snares for 8 sec, down from 9 sec.
Mastery: Frostburn (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/76613/#15589-15640) now scales from 150% of Spell Power, down from 250% of SP. Now also increases the damage done by your Water Elemental by 150% of your Spell Power.

Arcane

Arcane Charge (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/114664/#15589-15640) now also works with Arcane Explosion.
Slow (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/31589/#15589-15640) now increases casting time by 50% on creatures and 25% on players.

Fire

Combustion (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/11129/#15589-15640) base damage has been increased by 30%. No longer affected by Flamestrike effects on the target.
Inferno Blast (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/108853/#15589-15640) no longer affects Flamestrike effects. Now affects enemy targets within 10 yards, up from 8 yards.
Pyroblast (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/11366/#15589-15640) now requires single-target direct damage Fire spells to proc.

Minor Glyphs

Glyph of Arcane Language (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/57925/#15589-15640) - Your Arcane Brilliance spell allows you to comprehend your allies' racial languages.

Major Glyphs

Glyph of Combustion (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/56368/#15589-15640) now increases the direct damage of Combustion as well.


http://static.mmo-champion.com/mmoc/images/icons/imonks.gif Monk (Forums (http://www.mmo-champion.com/forums/341-Monk)))
Baseline

Blackout Kick (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/100784/#15589-15640) now costs 2 Chi, up from 1 Chi. Base damage increased by 20%.
Crackling Jade Lightning (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/117952/#15589-15640) now costs 1.5% of Base Mana, down from 3%. When dealing damage, you have a 15% chance to generate 1 Chi.
Detox (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/115450/#15589-15640) now removes Disease effects instead of Bleed effects.
Expel Harm (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/115072/#15589-15640) now costs 2.5% of Base Mana, down from 6%. Now Generates 1 Chi.
Fortifying Brew (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/115203/#15589-15640) now Increases your health by 100%, and reduces damage taken by 20%. Lasts 20 sec.
Grapple Weapon (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/117368/#15589-15640) now grabs non-ranged weapons. If you steal a better main-hand weapon, your damage or healing will be increased by 5% or damage taken reduced by 5%.
Healing Sphere (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/115460/#15589-15640) now costs 2% of Base Mana, up from 1.5% of Base Mana. Now is instant cast, down from 1.5 sec cast. Now has a 0.5 sec cooldown.

Dark Soul: Misery (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/113860/#15589-15640) - Passive removed.
Drain Soul (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/1120/#15589-15640) - Now costs 3% of Base Mana. Base damage decreased to 1,895, down from 2,526. If the target is at or below 20% health, Drain Soul causes double the normal damage and your periodic damage spells tick 100% faster.
Nightfall (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/108558/#15589-15640) - now has a 10% chance to proc, up from 4%. This effect cannot occur more than 5 times a minute.
Soulburn: Curse (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/103112/#15589-15640) - Now works in a 15 yd radius, up from 10.

Warlock - Major Glyphs

Glyph of Conflagrate (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/56235/#15589-15640) - Conflagrate gains a second charge, but reduces the snare by 20%.
Glyph of Demon Hunting (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/63303/#15589-15640) - Requires Demonology.
Glyph of Immolate (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/56228/#15589-15640) - Renamed Glyph of Dark Soul. While off cooldown, your Dark Soul ability passively grants you 10% of the active effect, but reduces the power of Dark Soul by 10%.
Glyph of Incinerate (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/56242/#15589-15640) - Renamed Glyph of Imp Swarm. Teaches you the ability Imp Swarm. Requires Demonology. Summons 5 Wild Imps; from the Twisting Nether to attack the target. The Wild Imps passive effect is disabled while Imp Swarm is on cooldown.
Glyph of Life Tap (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/63320/#15589-15640) - Your Life Tap no longer consumes health, but instead absorbs 15% of MHP healing recieved. This effect stacks. The absorb lasts 30 sec.
Glyph of Shadowflame (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/63310/#15589-15640) - Your Shadowflame slow is increased to 50% but Hand of Gul'dan no longer has charges.

Warlock - Minor Glyphs

Glyph of Bane of Agony (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/56241/#15589-15640) - Renamed Glyph of Verdant Spheres. Your Soul Shards are transformed into Verdant Spheres.
Glyph of Imp (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/56248/#15589-15640) - Renamed Glyph of Hand of Gul'dan. Your Hand of Gul'dan can now be targetted at a location.

Battle Stance (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/2457/#15589-15640) - Increases rage generated from normal melee attacks by 100%.
Berserker Rage (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/18499/#15589-15640) - You become Enraged, increasing the rage you generate from normal melee attacks by 50% for 6 sec.
Berserker Stance (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/2458/#15589-15640) - A reckless combat stance. Generates rage from damage taken.
Block (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/123829/#15589-15640) - New: Gives a chance to block enemy melee attacks.
Defensive Stance (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/71/#15589-15640) - A tanking combat stance. Decreases damage taken by 15%. Reduces the chance you will be critically hit by melee attacks by 6%. Significantly increases threat generation.
Enrage (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/13046/#15589-15640) - Now works with melee abilities instead of just special abilities. Now increases the rage you generate from normal melee attacks by 50% for 6 sec, up from 25%.
Spell Reflection (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/23920/#15589-15640) - Cooldown reduced to 15 sec, down from 25 sec.

Warrior - Talents

Enraged Regeneration (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/55694/#15589-15640) - Now costs 60 Rage. Costs no Rage if used while Enraged. Now heals over 5 secs, down from 10 secs.
Piercing Howl (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/12323/#15589-15640) - Duration increased to 15 sec, up from 6 sec.

Warrior - Arms

Die by the Sword (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/118038/#15589-15640) - Duration increased to 8 sec, up from 5 sec.
Mortal Strike (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/12294/#15589-15640) - Damage increased to 150% weapon damage, up from 125%.
Overpower (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/7384/#15589-15640) - Damage decreased to 120% weapon damage, down from 140%.
Sweeping Strikes (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/12328/#15589-15640) - Cooldown removed.

Warrior - Protection

Bastion of Defense (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/84608/#15589-15640) - Increases your block chance by 10%, down from 15%. No longer increases armor from items.
Revenge (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/6572/#15589-15640) - Cooldown reduced to 4.5 sec, down from 6 sec.
Shield Barrier (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/112048/#15589-15640) - Raise your shield, absorbing (100% of AP) damage for the next 6 sec. Absorption amount increases with attack power.
Unwavering Sentinel (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/29144/#15589-15640) - now increases armor value from items by 10% instead of reducing chances to be critically hit.

Warrior - Fury

Bloodthirst (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/23881/#15589-15640) - Damage decreased to 75% weapon damage, down from 100%. The chance for Bloodthirst to be a critical strike increases the longer it has been since you have been Enraged.
Meat Cleaver (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/12950/#15589-15640) - Dealing damage with Whirlwind reduces the Rage cost of your next Whirlwind by 5. This effect stacks up to 3 times.
Raging Blow (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/96103/#15589-15640) - Damage reduced to 120% weapon damage, down from 150%.
Single-Minded Fury (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/81099/#15589-15640) - When you dual-wield one-handed weapons, all damage is increased by 25% (was 35%), and your off-hand weapon will deal an additional 30% (was 40%) damage.
Whirlwind (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/1680/#15589-15640) - Rage cost increased to 30 rage, up from 25. Cooldown removed. Now deals 100% weapon damage, up from 35%.
Wild Strike (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/100130/#15589-15640) - Damage reduced to 220% weapon damage, down from 270%.

Warrior - Major Glyphs

Glyph of Incite (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/122013/#15589-15640) - Your Devastate hits cause your next Heroic Strike or Cleave to hit for 100% more damage.
Glyph of Sweeping Strikes (http://www.wowdb.com/spells/58384/#15589-15640) - Reduces the duration of Sweeping Strikes by 50%, but it hits one extra target.
